&lt;td style="width: 521.15pt; border: solid windowtext 3.0pt; padding: 0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt; height: 110.5pt;" valign="top" width="695"&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: center; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;" align="center"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt; font-family: 'Century Gothic',sans-serif;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;HTSB&amp;rsquo;s Mission and Vision&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;The HTSB envisions a highly esteemed Hawaiʻi public education system with rigorous professional teacher standards that foster student success. Our mission is to collaboratively set high teacher licensing and credentialing standards to:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 15.0pt; text-indent: -15.0pt; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;&amp;bull;&lt;span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;Provide every child in Hawaiʻi with qualified teachers.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 15.0pt; text-indent: -15.0pt; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;&amp;bull;&lt;span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;Promote professionalism and teaching excellence.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 15.0pt; text-indent: -15.0pt; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;&amp;bull;&lt;span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;Build public confidence in the teaching profession.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 15.0pt; text-indent: -15.0pt; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;&amp;bull;&lt;span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;Provide more accountability to the public.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10pt; text-indent: -15pt;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/td&gt;&#xD;

&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: center;" align="center"&gt;&lt;strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; letter-spacing: -.25pt;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;

&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;* &lt;u&gt;WRITTEN TESTIMONY:&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;The Hawaiʻi Teacher Standards Board (HTSB) welcomes public testimony on agenda items. Written testimony submitted and received at least 48 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8pt; text-indent: 4.5pt;"&gt;hours prior to the meeting will be posted on the Board&amp;rsquo;s website. Testimony sent to any other email address or testimony submitted after the meeting &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;start time, up to 24 hours after the meeting, will be processed as late testimony and will be posted after the meeting. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;Persons interested in submitting written public testimony shall &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: #222222; background: white;"&gt;submit testimony by one of the following methods&lt;strong&gt;:&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;ul&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Email to &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;&lt;a href="mailto:htsb@hawaii.gov"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: blue;"&gt;htsb@hawaii.gov&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt; as an attachment or written directly in your email message (please do not provide links to testimony)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;FAX to 808-586-2606&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Mail to HTSB, 650 Iwilei Road, Suite 268, Honolulu, HI 96817&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/ul&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="background: white; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt 4.5pt;"&gt;&lt;a name="_Hlk160732104"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8pt;"&gt;All testimony is permanently posted publicly on the HTSB&amp;rsquo;s website and referenced in the Board meeting minutes. Consider this when including personal information (including email addresses, phone numbers, names, and pictures) in your testimony.&amp;nbsp; If you want your personal information redacted, or omitted, submit your testimony as an attachment and include "NO PERSONAL INFORMATION" in the subject line.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent: -4.5pt; background: white; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt 9.0pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Indicate the following information on written testimony:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;ul&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Include "Testimony" in the subject line;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Name (or unique identifier) with position/title and organization, if applicable;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Meeting (name of committee or General Business meeting);&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Agenda item; and&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Position (support, oppose, or comment)&lt;/span&gt;​&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/ul&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;ONLINE TESTIMONY: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;Persons wishing to provide online testimony via Zoom must be logged in to Zoom using the same name they used to sign up for testimony. Testifiers shall use the Chat Box to provide their name and agenda item(s) they are testifying on. Testifiers will be called on and unmuted to give their testimony at the&lt;span style="letter-spacing: .05pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;appropriate&lt;span style="letter-spacing: .05pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;time&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.15pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;in the agenda. Testimony must be related to an item that is on the agenda. Each individual is allotted five minutes, or an amount of time otherwise designated by the Chairperson, to provide testimony to the Board and/or committee.&lt;span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"&gt;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;Y&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext; background: white;"&gt;ou may use a unique identifier (i.e., an alias) instead of your real name to maintain anonymity, but on the day of the meeting you&amp;nbsp;must&amp;nbsp;log into Zoom with the&amp;nbsp;same identifier&amp;nbsp;you used to sign up for testimony or you will not be unmuted. If you are testifying in-person, you must answer when your unique identifier is called.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt;MEETING MATERIALS:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt; To reduce costs, electronic materials are posted on the HTSB website,&lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href="file:///C:/Users/Kellianne/Downloads/%20https:/www.hawaiiteacherstandardsboard.org%20"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt; &lt;strong&gt;https://www.hawaiiteacherstandardsboard.org &lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: #444444;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt;The Board packet is available for inspection in the Board's office. For those who wish to have copies, the HTSB office will make copies of such materials at a cost of $0.25 per sheet, payable by check to HTSB.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;VIRTUAL MEETINGS:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt; Virtual meeting Zoom links can be found on the top of all agendas. Agendas can be found on the &lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href="https://www.hawaiiteacherstandardsboard.org/apps/pages/index.jsp?uREC_ID=4404111&amp;amp;type=d&amp;amp;pREC_ID=2643473"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;HTSB website&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;PUBLIC MEETING LOCATION:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;650 Iwilei Road, Suite 158, Honolulu, HI 96817&lt;strong&gt; &lt;/strong&gt;(Dole Cannery).&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt;ACCOMMODATIONS:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; color: #202020;"&gt;If you need an auxiliary aid, service, or other accommodation due to a disability, please contact the Board&amp;rsquo;s office at &lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href="mailto:htsb@hawaii.gov"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;htsb@hawaii.gov&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; color: #202020;"&gt; or (808) 784-5580 as soon as possible. Requests made as early as possible will give staff additional time to try to fulfill your request. Staff will try to fulfill all requests but cannot guarantee fulfillment.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="background: white;"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;PARKING:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;ul style="margin-top: 0in;" type="disc"&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo2; background: white; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Free parking: Dole Cannery Open-Air Parking Lot &amp;ndash; Free parking is available in the parking lot directly behind the Dole Cannery and adjacent to the Costco parking lot. The lot entry is from Alakawa Street.&amp;nbsp; There is no charge for parking in this free lot (2-hour limit).&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo2; background: white; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Pay parking: Dole Cannery Parking Structure &amp;ndash; Pay parking is available in the parking structure across Iwilei Road above the Regal Cinema theaters. The entrance is on Pacific Street.&amp;nbsp; You will pay for your parking when you exit the garage.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/ul&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;HTSB&amp;rsquo;s Mailing List:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href="http://eepurl.com/h7tW3j"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;Sign-up&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;to receive HTSB meeting agendas. Agendas are posted six calendar days in advance of the Board meetings.&lt;strong&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;

&lt;p class="TableParagraph" style="margin: 0.05pt 0in 0.0001pt 0.5in; text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;strong style="text-indent: -70.05pt;"&gt;Public&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.3pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;Meeting&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.15pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;Location:&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 2.0pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;650&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.25pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;Iwilei&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.1pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;Road,&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.2pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;Suite&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.2pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;158,&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.1pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;Honolulu,&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.1pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;HI&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 4.0pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;96817&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="TableParagraph" style="margin: 0.05pt 0in 0.0001pt 0.5in; text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;strong style="text-indent: -70.05pt;"&gt;Telephone: 808-784-5580 &amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; FAX: 808-586-2606&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;

&lt;tr style="height: 92px;"&gt;&#xD;
&lt;td style="width: 0%; border-width: medium 3pt 3pt; border-style: none solid solid; border-color: currentcolor black black; border-image: initial; padding: 0in; height: 92px;" colspan="3" valign="top" width="686"&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: center;" align="center"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;HTSB&amp;rsquo;s Mission and Vision&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;The HTSB envisions a highly esteemed Hawaiʻi public education system with rigorous professional teacher standards that foster student success. Our mission is to collaboratively set high teacher licensing and credentialing standards to:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 15.0pt; text-indent: -15.0pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;&amp;bull;&lt;span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;Provide every child in Hawaiʻi with qualified teachers.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 15.0pt; text-indent: -15.0pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;&amp;bull;&lt;span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;Promote professionalism and teaching excellence.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 15.0pt; text-indent: -15.0pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;&amp;bull;&lt;span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;Build public confidence in the teaching profession. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoListParagraph" style="margin-left: 16.35pt; text-indent: -16.35pt; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo6;"&gt;&lt;!-- [if !supportLists]--&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;"&gt;&lt;span style="mso-list: Ignore;"&gt;&amp;middot;&lt;span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;!--[endif]--&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;Provide more accountability to the public.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/td&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/tr&gt;&#xD;

&lt;p class="MsoBodyText" style="margin: .4pt 0in .0001pt 0in;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 3.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 8.0pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;* &lt;u&gt;WRITTEN TESTIMONY:&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8pt; text-indent: 4.5pt;"&gt;The Hawaiʻi Teacher Standards Board (HTSB) welcomes public testimony on agenda items. Written testimony submitted and received at least 48 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;hours prior to the meeting will be posted on the Board&amp;rsquo;s website. Testimony sent to any other email address or testimony submitted after the meeting &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8pt; text-indent: 4.5pt;"&gt;start time, up to 24 hours after the meeting, will be processed as late testimony and will be posted after the meeting.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;Persons interested in submitting written public testimony shall &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: #222222; background: white;"&gt;submit testimony by one of the following methods&lt;strong&gt;:&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;ul&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Email to &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;&lt;a href="mailto:htsb@hawaii.gov"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: blue;"&gt;htsb@hawaii.gov&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt; as an attachment or written directly in your email message (please do not provide links to testimony)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;FAX to 808-586-2606&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Mail to HTSB, 650 Iwilei Road, Suite 268, Honolulu, HI 96817&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/ul&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="background: white; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt 4.5pt;"&gt;&lt;a name="_Hlk160732104"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8pt;"&gt;All testimony is permanently posted publicly on the HTSB&amp;rsquo;s website and referenced in the Board meeting minutes. Consider this when including personal information (including email addresses, phone numbers, names, and pictures) in your testimony.&amp;nbsp; If you want your personal information redacted, or omitted, submit your testimony as an attachment and include "NO PERSONAL INFORMATION" in the subject line.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent: -4.5pt; background: white; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt 9.0pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Indicate the following information on written testimony:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;ul&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Include "Testimony" in the subject line;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Name (or unique identifier) with position/title and organization, if applicable;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Meeting (name of committee or General Business meeting);&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Agenda item; and&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Position (support, oppose, or comment)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/ul&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Raleway; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext; background: white;"&gt;​&lt;/span&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;ONLINE TESTIMONY:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;Persons wishing to provide online testimony via Zoom must be logged in to Zoom using the same name they used to sign up for testimony. Testifiers shall use the Chat Box to provide their name and agenda item(s) they are testifying on. Testifiers will be called on and unmuted to give their testimony at the&lt;span style="letter-spacing: .05pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;appropriate&lt;span style="letter-spacing: .05pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;time&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.15pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;in the agenda. Testimony must be related to an item that is on the agenda. Each individual is allotted five minutes, or an amount of time otherwise designated by the Chairperson, to provide testimony to the Board and/or committee.&lt;span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"&gt;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext; background: white;"&gt;You may use a unique identifier (i.e., an alias) instead of your real name to maintain anonymity, but on the day of the meeting you&amp;nbsp;must&amp;nbsp;log into Zoom with the&amp;nbsp;same identifier&amp;nbsp;you used to sign up for testimony or you will not be unmuted. If you are testifying in-person, you must answer when your unique identifier is called.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt;MEETING MATERIALS:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt; To reduce costs, electronic materials are posted on the HTSB website,&lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href="https://www.hawaiiteacherstandardsboard.org/"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: blue;"&gt;https://www.hawaiiteacherstandardsboard.org&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: #444444;"&gt;&lt;span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt;The Board packet is available for inspection in the Board's office. For those who wish to have copies, the HTSB office will make copies of such materials at a cost of $0.25 per sheet, payable by check to HTSB.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;VIRTUAL MEETINGS:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt; Virtual meeting Zoom links can be found on the top of all agendas. Agendas can be found on the &lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href="https://www.hawaiiteacherstandardsboard.org/apps/pages/index.jsp?uREC_ID=4404111&amp;amp;type=d&amp;amp;pREC_ID=2643473"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;HTSB website&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span class="MsoHyperlink"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;PUBLIC MEETING LOCATION:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;650 Iwilei Road, Suite 158, Honolulu, HI 96817&lt;strong&gt; &lt;/strong&gt;(Dole Cannery).&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt;ACCOMMODATIONS:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; font-family: 'Arial',sans-serif; color: #202020;"&gt;If you need an auxiliary aid, service, or other accommodation due to a disability, please contact the Board&amp;rsquo;s office at &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;a href="mailto:htsb@hawaii.gov"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;htsb@hawaii.gov&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; font-family: 'Arial',sans-serif; color: #202020;"&gt; or (808) 784-5580 as soon as possible. Requests made as early as possible will give staff additional time to try to fulfill your request. Staff will try to fulfill all requests but cannot guarantee fulfillment.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="background: white;"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;PARKING:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;ul style="margin-top: 0in;" type="disc"&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo1; background: white; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Free parking: Dole Cannery Open-Air Parking Lot &amp;ndash; Free parking is available in the parking lot directly behind the Dole Cannery and adjacent to the Costco parking lot. The lot entry is from Alakawa Street.&amp;nbsp; There is no charge for parking in this free lot (2-hour limit).&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/ul&gt;&#xD;
&lt;ul style="margin-top: 0in;" type="disc"&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo1; background: white; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Pay parking: Dole Cannery Parking Structure &amp;ndash; Pay parking is available in the parking structure across Iwilei Road above the Regal Cinema theaters. The entrance is on Pacific Street.&amp;nbsp; You will pay for your parking when you exit the garage.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/ul&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;HTSB&amp;rsquo;s Mailing List:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href="http://eepurl.com/h7tW3j"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;Sign-up&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; font-family: 'Arial',sans-serif;"&gt; to receive HTSB meeting agendas. Agendas are posted six calendar days in advance of the Board meetings.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;

&lt;p class="TableParagraph" style="text-align: center; text-indent: -.15pt; margin: 3.85pt 135.25pt .0001pt 155.45pt;" align="center"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;

&lt;p class="TableParagraph" style="text-align: center; margin: 0in 191.8pt .0001pt 0in;" align="center"&gt;&lt;strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.45pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;11:00 AM &lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="TableParagraph" style="text-align: center; margin: 0in 191.8pt .0001pt 0in;" align="center"&gt;&lt;strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"&gt;&lt;span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.1pt;"&gt;Agenda&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="TableParagraph" style="text-align: center; margin: 0in 191.8pt .0001pt 0in;" align="center"&gt;&lt;strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="TableParagraph" style="margin: .05pt 0in .0001pt 1.5in;"&gt;&lt;strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"&gt;Join&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.15pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;Zoom&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.2pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;Meeting: &lt;/strong&gt;&lt;a href="https://us06web.zoom.us/j/88697112727"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;https://us06web.zoom.us/j/88697112727&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;strong&gt; &lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="TableParagraph" style="margin: .05pt 0in .0001pt 1.5in;"&gt;&lt;strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="TableParagraph" style="margin: .05pt 0in .0001pt 1.5in;"&gt;&lt;strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"&gt;Meeting&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.35pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;ID: 886 9711 2727;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.2pt;"&gt; &lt;span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Passcode: 191520 &lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="TableParagraph" style="text-indent: -70.05pt; line-height: 25.3pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly; tab-stops: 288.4pt; margin: .75pt 35.75pt .0001pt 124.45pt;"&gt;&lt;strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"&gt;Public&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.3pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;Meeting&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.15pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;Location:&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 2.0pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;650&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.25pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;Iwilei&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.1pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;Road,&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.2pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;Suite&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.2pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;158,&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.1pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;Honolulu,&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.1pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;HI&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 4.0pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;96817 Telephone: 808-784-5580&lt;span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;FAX: 808-586-2606&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border-collapse: collapse; mso-table-layout-alt: fixed; border: none; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext 3.0pt; mso-yfti-tbllook: 1184; mso-padding-alt: 0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt; mso-border-insideh: 3.0pt solid windowtext; mso-border-insidev: 3.0pt solid windowtext;" border="1" width="695" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"&gt;&#xD;
&lt;tbody&gt;&#xD;
&lt;tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 0; mso-yfti-firstrow: yes; mso-yfti-lastrow: yes; height: 109.5pt;"&gt;&#xD;
&lt;td style="width: 521.15pt; border: solid windowtext 3.0pt; padding: 0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt; height: 109.5pt;" valign="top" width="695"&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: center; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;" align="center"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt; font-family: 'Century Gothic',sans-serif;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;HTSB&amp;rsquo;s Mission and Vision&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;The HTSB envisions a highly esteemed Hawaiʻi public education system with rigorous professional teacher standards that foster student success. Our mission is to collaboratively set high teacher licensing and credentialing standards to:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 15.0pt; text-indent: -15.0pt; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;&amp;bull;&lt;span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;Provide every child in Hawaiʻi with qualified teachers.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 15.0pt; text-indent: -15.0pt; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;&amp;bull;&lt;span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;Promote professionalism and teaching excellence.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 15.0pt; text-indent: -15.0pt; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;&amp;bull;&lt;span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;Build public confidence in the teaching profession.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 15.0pt; text-indent: -15.0pt; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;&amp;bull;&lt;span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;Provide more accountability to the public.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/td&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/tr&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/tbody&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/table&gt;&#xD;

&lt;p class="MsoBodyText" style="margin: .4pt 0in .0001pt 0in;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 3.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 8.0pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;* &lt;u&gt;WRITTEN TESTIMONY:&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8pt; text-indent: 4.5pt;"&gt;The Hawaiʻi Teacher Standards Board (HTSB) welcomes public testimony on agenda items. Written testimony submitted and received at least 48 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8pt; text-indent: 4.5pt;"&gt;hours prior to the meeting will be posted on the Board&amp;rsquo;s website. Testimony sent to any other email address or testimony submitted after the meeting &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8pt; text-indent: 4.5pt;"&gt;start time, up to 24 hours after the meeting, will be processed as late testimony and will be posted after the meeting.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8pt; text-indent: 4.5pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;span style="text-indent: 4.5pt; font-size: 8pt;"&gt;Persons interested in submitting written public testimony shall &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="text-indent: 4.5pt; font-size: 8pt; color: #222222; background: white;"&gt;submit testimony by one of the following methods&lt;strong&gt;:&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;ul&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Email to &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;&lt;a href="mailto:htsb@hawaii.gov"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: blue;"&gt;htsb@hawaii.gov&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt; as an attachment or written directly in your email message (please do not provide links to testimony)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;FAX to 808-586-2606&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Mail to HTSB, 650 Iwilei Road, Suite 268, Honolulu, HI 96817&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/ul&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="background: white; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt 4.5pt;"&gt;&lt;a name="_Hlk160732104"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8pt;"&gt;All testimony is permanently posted publicly on the HTSB&amp;rsquo;s website and referenced in the Board meeting minutes. Consider this when including personal information (including email addresses, phone numbers, names, and pictures) in your testimony.&amp;nbsp; If you want your personal information redacted, or omitted, submit your testimony as an attachment and include "NO PERSONAL INFORMATION" in the subject line.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent: -4.5pt; background: white; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt 9.0pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Indicate the following information on written testimony:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;ul&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Include "Testimony" in the subject line;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Name (or unique identifier) with position/title and organization, if applicable;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Meeting (name of committee or General Business meeting);&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Agenda item; and&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Position (support, oppose, or comment)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/ul&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Raleway; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext; background: white;"&gt;​&lt;/span&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;ONLINE TESTIMONY:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;Persons wishing to provide online testimony via Zoom must be logged in to Zoom using the same name they used to sign up for testimony. Testifiers shall use the Chat Box to provide their name and agenda item(s) they are testifying on. Testifiers will be called on and unmuted to give their testimony at the&lt;span style="letter-spacing: .05pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;appropriate&lt;span style="letter-spacing: .05pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;time&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.15pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;in the agenda. Testimony must be related to an item that is on the agenda. Each individual is allotted five minutes, or an amount of time otherwise designated by the Chairperson, to provide testimony to the Board and/or committee.&lt;span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"&gt;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;Y&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext; background: white;"&gt;ou may use a unique identifier (i.e., an alias) instead of your real name to maintain anonymity, but on the day of the meeting you&amp;nbsp;must&amp;nbsp;log into Zoom with the&amp;nbsp;same identifier&amp;nbsp;you used to sign up for testimony or you will not be unmuted. If you are testifying in-person, you must answer when your unique identifier is called.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt;MEETING MATERIALS:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt; To reduce costs, electronic materials are posted on the HTSB website,&lt;strong&gt; &lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href="https://www.hawaiiteacherstandardsboard.org/"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt;https://www.hawaiiteacherstandardsboard.org/&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: #444444;"&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: #444444;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt;The Board packet is available for inspection in the Board's office. For those who wish to have copies, the HTSB office will make copies of such materials at a cost of $0.25 per sheet, payable by check to HTSB.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;VIRTUAL MEETINGS:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt; Virtual meeting Zoom links can be found on the top of all agendas. Agendas can be found on the &lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href="https://www.hawaiiteacherstandardsboard.org/apps/pages/index.jsp?uREC_ID=4404111&amp;amp;type=d&amp;amp;pREC_ID=2643473"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;HTSB website&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span class="MsoHyperlink"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;PUBLIC MEETING LOCATION:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;650 Iwilei Road, Suite 158, Honolulu, HI 96817&lt;strong&gt; &lt;/strong&gt;(Dole Cannery).&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt;ACCOMMODATIONS:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; font-family: 'Arial',sans-serif; color: #202020;"&gt;If you need an auxiliary aid, service, or other accommodation due to a disability, please contact the Board&amp;rsquo;s office at &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;a href="mailto:htsb@hawaii.gov"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;htsb@hawaii.gov&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; font-family: 'Arial',sans-serif; color: #202020;"&gt; or (808) 784-5580 as soon as possible. Requests made as early as possible will give staff additional time to try to fulfill your request. Staff will try to fulfill all requests but cannot guarantee fulfillment.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="background: white;"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;PARKING:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;ul style="margin-top: 0in;" type="disc"&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-list: l3 level1 lfo2; background: white; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Free parking: Dole Cannery Open-Air Parking Lot &amp;ndash; Free parking is available in the parking lot directly behind the Dole Cannery and adjacent to the Costco parking lot. The lot entry is from Alakawa Street.&amp;nbsp; There is no charge for parking in this free lot (2-hour limit).&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/ul&gt;&#xD;
&lt;ul style="margin-top: 0in;" type="disc"&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-list: l3 level1 lfo2; background: white; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Pay parking: Dole Cannery Parking Structure &amp;ndash; Pay parking is available in the parking structure across Iwilei Road above the Regal Cinema theaters. The entrance is on Pacific Street.&amp;nbsp; You will pay for your parking when you exit the garage.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/ul&gt;&#xD;

Agendas are posted six calendar days in advance of the Board meetings.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;

&lt;p class="TableParagraph" style="text-align: center; margin: 0in 191.8pt .0001pt 194.85pt;" align="center"&gt;&lt;strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;

&lt;p class="TableParagraph" style="margin: .5pt 0in .0001pt 0in;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="TableParagraph" style="margin-top: .05pt;"&gt;&lt;strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"&gt;&lt;span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;Join&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.15pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;Zoom&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.2pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;Meeting:&lt;/strong&gt; &lt;a href="https://us06web.zoom.us/j/83984040573"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;https://us06web.zoom.us/j/83984040573&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&amp;nbsp; &amp;nbsp; &amp;nbsp; &amp;nbsp; &amp;nbsp; &amp;nbsp; &amp;nbsp; &amp;nbsp; &amp;nbsp; &amp;nbsp; &amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="TableParagraph" style="margin-top: .05pt; text-align: center;" align="center"&gt;&lt;strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"&gt;Meeting&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.35pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;ID: 839 8404 0573;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.2pt;"&gt; &lt;span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Passcode: 053159 &lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="TableParagraph" style="text-indent: -70.05pt; line-height: 25.3pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly; tab-stops: 288.4pt; margin: .75pt 64.45pt .0001pt 124.45pt;"&gt;&lt;strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"&gt;Public&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.3pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;Meeting&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.15pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;Location:&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 2.0pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;650&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.25pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;Iwilei&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.1pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;Road,&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.2pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;Suite&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.2pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;158,&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.1pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;Honolulu,&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.1pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;HI&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 4.0pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;96817 Telephone: 808-784-5580&lt;span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;FAX: 808-586-2606&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border-collapse: collapse; mso-table-layout-alt: fixed; border: none; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext 3.0pt; mso-yfti-tbllook: 1184; mso-padding-alt: 0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt; mso-border-insideh: 3.0pt solid windowtext; mso-border-insidev: 3.0pt solid windowtext;" border="1" width="695" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"&gt;&#xD;
&lt;tbody&gt;&#xD;
&lt;tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 0; mso-yfti-firstrow: yes; mso-yfti-lastrow: yes; height: 109.5pt;"&gt;&#xD;
&lt;td style="width: 521.15pt; border: solid windowtext 3.0pt; padding: 0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt; height: 109.5pt;" valign="top" width="695"&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: center; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;" align="center"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt; font-family: 'Century Gothic',sans-serif;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;HTSB&amp;rsquo;s Mission and Vision&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;The HTSB envisions a highly esteemed Hawaiʻi public education system with rigorous professional teacher standards that foster student success. Our mission is to collaboratively set high teacher licensing and credentialing standards to:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 15.0pt; text-indent: -15.0pt; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;&amp;bull;&lt;span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;Provide every child in Hawaiʻi with qualified teachers.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 15.0pt; text-indent: -15.0pt; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;&amp;bull;&lt;span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;Promote professionalism and teaching excellence.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 15.0pt; text-indent: -15.0pt; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;&amp;bull;&lt;span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;Build public confidence in the teaching profession.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 15.0pt; text-indent: -15.0pt; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"&gt;&amp;bull;&lt;span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;Provide more accountability to the public.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/td&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/tr&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/tbody&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/table&gt;&#xD;

&lt;p class="TableParagraph" style="margin-left: 5.3pt; line-height: 9.55pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly;"&gt;&lt;strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"&gt;12:30 PM&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;

&lt;td style="width: 414.85pt; border-top: none; border-left: none; border-bottom: solid black 3.0pt; border-right: solid black 1.0pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid black .75pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid black .75pt; mso-border-alt: solid black .75pt; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid black 3.0pt; padding: 0in 0in 0in 0in; height: 12.75pt;" valign="top" width="553"&gt;&#xD;

&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: .5in; mso-add-space: auto; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 75.5pt; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;a Teaching Field Programs in Early Childhood Education&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: .5in; mso-add-space: auto; text-indent: -.25in; line-height: 115%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-list: l2 level1 lfo5; tab-stops: 75.5pt; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;!-- [if !supportLists]--&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;span style="mso-list: Ignore;"&gt;I.&lt;span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;!--[endif]--&gt;&lt;a href="https://media.edlio.net/e045d0de/98e02110/15c089e9/369aead331514f7da9358c32fadaf2ed?_=NBI%2025_49_Program%20Mod%20of%20UHM%20Literacy%20Specialist%20Program.pdf"&gt;&lt;strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri;"&gt;NBI 25-49&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri; color: red;"&gt;&lt;span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"&gt;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"&gt;Approval of Modifications to the University of Hawaiʻi at Mānoa&amp;rsquo;s Literacy &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: .25in; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 75.5pt; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;Specialist Add a Teaching Field Program&lt;span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"&gt;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 5.5pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-indent: 4.5pt; line-height: 115%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 115%;"&gt;IV.&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 2.55pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.1pt;"&gt;Adjournment&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/td&gt;&#xD;
&lt;td style="width: 49.5pt; border-top: none; border-left: none; border-bottom: solid black 3.0pt; border-right: solid black 3.0pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid black .75pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid black .75pt; padding: 0in 0in 0in 0in; height: 12.75pt;" valign="top" width="66"&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="TableParagraph" style="margin-left: 5.4pt; line-height: 9.55pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly;"&gt;&lt;strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; letter-spacing: -.1pt;"&gt;Gillentine&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;

&lt;p class="MsoBodyText" style="margin: .4pt 0in .0001pt 0in;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 3.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 8.0pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;* &lt;u&gt;WRITTEN TESTIMONY:&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8pt; text-indent: -9pt;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8pt; text-indent: -9pt;"&gt;The Hawaiʻi Teacher Standards Board (HTSB) welcomes public testimony on agenda items. Written testimony submitted and received at least 48 hours prior to the meeting will be posted on the Board&amp;rsquo;s website. Testimony sent to any other email address or testimony submitted after the meeting start time, up to 24 hours after the meeting, will be processed as late testimony and will be posted after the meeting.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;Persons interested in submitting written public testimony shall &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: #222222; background: white;"&gt;submit testimony by one of the following methods:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;ul&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Email to &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;&lt;a href="mailto:htsb@hawaii.gov"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: blue;"&gt;htsb@hawaii.gov&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt; as an attachment or written directly in your email message (please do not provide links to testimony)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;FAX to 808-586-2606&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Mail to HTSB, 650 Iwilei Road, Suite 268, Honolulu, HI 96817&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/ul&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="background: white; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt 9.0pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;All testimony is permanently posted publicly on the HTSB&amp;rsquo;s website and referenced in the Board meeting minutes. Consider this when including personal information (including email addresses, phone numbers, names, and pictures) in your testimony.&lt;span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"&gt;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;If you want your personal information redacted or omitted, submit your testimony as an attachment and include "NO PERSONAL INFORMATION" in the subject line.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 7.5pt; background: white;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;&lt;span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;Indicate the following information on written testimony:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;ul&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Include "Testimony" in the subject line;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Name (or unique identifier) with position/title and organization, if applicable;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Meeting (name of committee or General Business meeting);&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Agenda item; and&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Position (support, oppose, or comment)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/ul&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Raleway; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext; background: white;"&gt;​&lt;/span&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;ONLINE TESTIMONY:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;Persons wishing to provide online testimony via Zoom must be logged in to Zoom using the same name they used to sign up for testimony. Testifiers shall use the Chat Box to provide their name and agenda item(s) they are testifying on. Testifiers will be called on and unmuted to give their testimony at the&lt;span style="letter-spacing: .05pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;appropriate&lt;span style="letter-spacing: .05pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;time&lt;span style="letter-spacing: -.15pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;in the agenda. Testimony must be related to an item that is on the agenda. Each individual is allotted five minutes, or an amount of time otherwise designated by the Chairperson, to provide testimony to the Board and/or committee.&lt;span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8pt;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext; background: white;"&gt;You may use a unique identifier (i.e., an alias) instead of your real name to maintain anonymity, but on the day of the meeting you&amp;nbsp;must&amp;nbsp;log into Zoom with the&amp;nbsp;same identifier&amp;nbsp;you used to sign up for testimony or you will not be unmuted. If you are testifying in-person, you must answer when your unique identifier is called.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt;MEETING MATERIALS:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt; To reduce costs, electronic materials are posted on the HTSB website,&lt;strong&gt; &lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href="https://www.hawaiiteacherstandardsboard.org/"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt;https://www.hawaiiteacherstandardsboard.org/&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: #444444;"&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: #444444;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt;The Board packet is available for inspection in the Board's office. For those who wish to have copies, the HTSB office will make copies of such materials at a cost of $0.25 per sheet, payable by check to HTSB.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;VIRTUAL MEETINGS:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt; Virtual meeting Zoom links can be found on the top of all agendas. Agendas can be found on the &lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href="https://www.hawaiiteacherstandardsboard.org/apps/pages/index.jsp?uREC_ID=4404111&amp;amp;type=d&amp;amp;pREC_ID=2643473"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;HTSB website&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span class="MsoHyperlink"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;"&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;PUBLIC MEETING LOCATION:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;650 Iwilei Road, Suite 158, Honolulu, HI 96817&lt;strong&gt; &lt;/strong&gt;(Dole Cannery).&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt;ACCOMMODATIONS:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; font-family: 'Arial',sans-serif; color: #202020;"&gt;If you need an auxiliary aid, service, or other accommodation due to a disability, please contact the Board&amp;rsquo;s office at &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;a href="mailto:htsb@hawaii.gov"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt;"&gt;htsb@hawaii.gov&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; font-family: 'Arial',sans-serif; color: #202020;"&gt; or (808) 784-5580 as soon as possible. Requests made as early as possible will give staff additional time to try to fulfill your request. Staff will try to fulfill all requests but cannot guarantee fulfillment.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="background: white;"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;PARKING:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;ul style="margin-top: 0in;" type="disc"&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-list: l3 level1 lfo2; background: white; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Free parking: Dole Cannery Open-Air Parking Lot &amp;ndash; Free parking is available in the parking lot directly behind the Dole Cannery and adjacent to the Costco parking lot. The lot entry is from Alakawa Street.&amp;nbsp; There is no charge for parking in this free lot (2-hour limit).&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/ul&gt;&#xD;
&lt;ul style="margin-top: 0in;" type="disc"&gt;&#xD;
&lt;li class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-list: l3 level1 lfo2; background: white; text-autospace: ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 8.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: black; mso-color-alt: windowtext;"&gt;Pay parking: Dole Cannery Parking Structure &amp;ndash; Pay parking is available in the parking structure across Iwilei Road above the Regal Cinema theaters. The entrance is on Pacific Street.&amp;nbsp; You will pay for your parking when you exit the garage.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/ul&gt;&#xD;

Agendas are posted six calendar days in advance of the Board meetings.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;

&lt;td style="width: 515.1pt; border-width: 3pt; border-color: windowtext; padding: 0in 5.4pt; height: 106.8pt;" valign="top" width="687"&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: center; line-height: normal;" align="center"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt; font-family: 'Arial',sans-serif;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt; font-family: 'Arial',sans-serif;"&gt;HTSB&amp;rsquo;s Mission and Vision&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt; font-family: 'Arial',sans-serif;"&gt;:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0in; line-height: normal;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt; font-family: 'Arial',sans-serif;"&gt;The HTSB envisions a highly esteemed Hawaiʻi public education system with rigorous professional teacher standards that foster student success. Our mission is to collaboratively set high teacher licensing and credentialing standards to:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent: -15.0pt; line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0in 15.0pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt; font-family: 'Arial',sans-serif;"&gt;&amp;bull;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; Provide every child in Hawaiʻi with qualified teachers.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent: -15.0pt; line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0in 15.0pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt; font-family: 'Arial',sans-serif;"&gt;&amp;bull;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; Promote professionalism and teaching excellence.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent: -15.0pt; line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0in 15.0pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt; font-family: 'Arial',sans-serif;"&gt;&amp;bull;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; Build public confidence in the teaching profession.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent: -15.0pt; line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0in 15.0pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%; font-family: 'Arial',sans-serif;"&gt;&amp;bull;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; Provide more accountability to the public.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;/td&gt;&#xD;

&lt;p class="Informal1" style="mso-add-space: auto; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l2 level2 lfo2; margin: 0in 26.5pt 0in 35.3pt;"&gt;&lt;!-- [if !supportLists]--&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: Arial, sans-serif;"&gt;E.&lt;span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;!--[endif]--&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: Arial, sans-serif;"&gt;The purpose of this agenda item is to discuss the appropriate action to be taken on NBI 25-34; Case No. 24-05 pursuant to &lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href="https://acrobat.adobe.com/id/urn:aaid:sc:va6c2:a1cb0fb1-8bfe-4314-b90d-af0c514f6cdc"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9.0pt; font-family: 'Arial',sans-serif;"&gt;HRS&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: Arial, sans-serif;"&gt; &amp;sect;92-5(a)(1). &lt;p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst" style="mso-add-space: auto; text-indent: -.25in; line-height: normal; mso-list: l2 level2 lfo2; margin: 3.0pt 0in 0in 35.25pt;"&gt;&lt;!-- [if !supportLists]--&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: Arial, sans-serif;"&gt;F.&lt;span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;!--[endif]--&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: Arial, sans-serif;"&gt;The purpose of this agenda item is to discuss &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: Arial, sans-serif;"&gt;the appropriate action to take on NBI 25-35; Case No. 25-07 pursuant to &lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href="https://acrobat.adobe.com/id/urn:aaid:sc:va6c2:a1cb0fb1-8bfe-4314-b90d-af0c514f6cdc"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9.0pt; font-family: 'Arial',sans-serif; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt;Hawaii Administrative Rules&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: Arial, sans-serif;"&gt; &amp;sect;8-54-16 Suspension of the rules.&amp;nbsp; The educator is seeking to have the Board suspend the rules pertaining to the criteria needed to be issued a Fourth Emergency Hire Permit due to extenuating circumstances caused by the educator preparation program.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="mso-add-space: auto; text-indent: -.25in; line-height: normal; mso-list: l2 level2 lfo2; margin: 3.0pt 0in 0in 35.25pt;"&gt;&lt;!-- [if !supportLists]--&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: Arial, sans-serif;"&gt;G.&lt;span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;!--[endif]--&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: Arial, sans-serif;"&gt;The purpose of this agenda item is to discuss the appropriate action to take on NBI 25-50; Case No. 25-08, pursuant to &lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href="https://acrobat.adobe.com/id/urn:aaid:sc:va6c2:a1cb0fb1-8bfe-4314-b90d-af0c514f6cdc"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9.0pt; font-family: 'Arial',sans-serif;"&gt;Hawaii Revised Statutes&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: Arial, sans-serif;"&gt; &amp;sect;92-5(a)(1), regarding the request by the educator to be issued a fourth Emergency Hire Permit and to suspend the Board&amp;rsquo;s administrative rules based on extenuating circumstances caused by family tragedy, a tragedy at educator&amp;rsquo;s school, and constraints in course scheduling.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
&lt;p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="mso-add-space: auto; text-indent: -.25in; line-height: normal; mso-list: l2 level2 lfo2; margin: 3.0pt 0in 0in 35.25pt;"&gt;&lt;!-- [if !supportLists]--&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: Arial, sans-serif;"&gt;H.&lt;span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-family: 'Times New Roman';"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;!--[endif]--&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: Arial, sans-serif;"&gt;The purpose of this agenda item is to discuss the appropriate action to take on NBI 25-51; Case No. 25-09, pursuant to &lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href="https://acrobat.adobe.com/id/urn:aaid:sc:va6c2:a1cb0fb1-8bfe-4314-b90d-af0c514f6cdc"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9.0pt; font-family: 'Arial',sans-serif;"&gt;Hawaii Revised Statutes &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: Arial, sans-serif;"&gt;&amp;sect;92-5(a)(1), regarding this educator&amp;rsquo;s application for renewal of the educator&amp;rsquo;s Standard License. In this case, the educator was terminated for noncompliance of the Hawaiʻi Department of Education&amp;rsquo;s COVID-19 Testing Attestation Mandate and did not file a grievance with the educator&amp;rsquo;s union regarding the termination. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#xD;
